\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Copyright\ (c)\ Electronic\ Arts\ Inc.\ All\ rights\ reserved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ file\ implements\ a\ vector\ (array-\/like\ container),\ much\ like\ the\ C++}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ std::vector\ class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ primary\ distinctions\ between\ this\ vector\ and\ std::vector\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ has\ a\ couple\ extension\ functions\ that\ increase\ performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ can\ contain\ objects\ with\ alignment\ requirements.\ std::vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ cannot\ do\ so\ without\ a\ bit\ of\ tedious\ non-\/portable\ effort.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ supports\ debug\ memory\ naming\ natively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ is\ easier\ to\ read,\ debug,\ and\ visualize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ is\ savvy\ to\ an\ environment\ that\ doesn't\ have\ exception\ handling,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ as\ is\ sometimes\ the\ case\ with\ console\ or\ embedded\ environments.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ has\ less\ deeply\ nested\ function\ calls\ and\ allows\ the\ user\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ enable\ forced\ inlining\ in\ debug\ builds\ in\ order\ to\ reduce\ bloat.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector<bool>\ is\ a\ vector\ of\ boolean\ values\ and\ not\ a\ bit\ vector.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ guarantees\ that\ memory\ is\ contiguous\ and\ that\ vector::iterator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ is\ nothing\ more\ than\ a\ pointer\ to\ T.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ has\ an\ explicit\ data()\ method\ for\ obtaining\ a\ pointer\ to\ storage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ which\ is\ safe\ to\ call\ even\ if\ the\ block\ is\ empty.\ This\ avoids\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ common\ \&v[0],\ \&v.front(),\ and\ \&*v.begin()\ constructs\ that\ trigger\ false}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ asserts\ in\ STL\ debugging\ modes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ data\ is\ guaranteed\ to\ be\ contiguous.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ vector\ has\ a\ set\_capacity()\ function\ which\ frees\ excess\ capacity.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ The\ only\ way\ to\ do\ this\ with\ std::vector\ is\ via\ the\ cryptic\ non-\/obvious}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ trick\ of\ using:\ vector<SomeClass>(x).swap(x);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ }
